③ Article Analysis · Minggu 13

Analisis Artikel 26 — Westermann-Behaylo, Van Buren III & Berman (2016)

Judul lengkap: Stakeholder Capability Enhancement as a Path to Promote Human Dignity and Cooperative Advantage. Penulis: Michelle K. Westermann-Behaylo, Harry J. Van Buren III, Shawn L. Berman. Publikasi: Business Horizons, Vol. 59 No. 1 (Jan-Feb 2016), pp. 79–88. Tipe riset: konseptual—integrasi teoritis.

Catatan Sumber Primer

PDF artikel tidak disediakan. Analisis disusun dari abstrak publik + literatur kanonik tentang capability approach (Sen 1999, 2009; Nussbaum 2011), stakeholder theory (Freeman 1984; Donaldson & Preston 1995; Mitchell et al. 1997), dan cooperative strategy (Dyer & Singh 1998). Mahasiswa dianjurkan mencari PDF asli untuk pendalaman.

Pertanyaan Riset / Kontribusi

Bagaimana perusahaan dapat mengintegrasikan ethical imperative untuk menghormati human dignity dengan strategic imperative untuk menciptakan competitive advantage? Artikel ini mengusulkan kerangka integratif: stakeholder capability enhancement sebagai path yang simultaneously promote human dignity DAN menghasilkan cooperative advantage.

Background Teoretis

1. Sen's Capability Approach

Amartya Sen (Nobel Economics 1998) mengembangkan capability approach sebagai alternative untuk utilitarian (sum of utility) dan resource-based (Rawlsian primary goods) conceptions of welfare. Inti: kesejahteraan manusia diukur dari capabilities (freedoms to achieve) bukan dari resources atau utility.

Nussbaum (2011) extend ini dengan list of central capabilities: life, bodily health, bodily integrity, senses-imagination-thought, emotions, practical reason, affiliation, other species, play, control over environment.

2. Stakeholder Theory

Freeman (1984): stakeholders adalah entities yang can affect or are affected by organization. Donaldson & Preston (1995): stakeholder theory memiliki tiga dimensi—descriptive, instrumental, normative. Berman et al. (1999): stakeholder management dapat bersumber dari strategic concerns (instrumental) atau moral commitments (normative).

3. Cooperative Strategy

Dyer & Singh (1998) memperkenalkan relational view: competitive advantage dapat bersumber dari relationships dengan specific partners (supply chain partners, alliances, customers). Ini menambah lens beyond industry-based (Porter) dan resource-based (Barney).

Argumen Utama

Westermann-Behaylo et al. mengintegrasikan ketiga tradisi untuk argue:

Proposisi 1 — Enhanced Capabilities = Enhanced Human Dignity

Human dignity bukan konsep abstrak—ia concrete ketika orang memiliki capabilities to pursue valued functionings. Perusahaan yang enhances stakeholder capabilities (skills training, economic opportunity, health access, dsb.) secara langsung promote human dignity.

Proposisi 2 — Enhanced Capabilities = Cooperative Advantage

Stakeholder dengan enhanced capabilities menjadi partners yang lebih capable: suppliers yang lebih produktif, employees yang lebih skilled, customers yang lebih loyal, communities yang lebih supportive. Relationships yang terbentuk melalui capability enhancement menciptakan cooperative advantage—value yang co-created yang sulit direplikasi.

Proposisi 3 — Human Dignity and Cooperative Advantage are Reinforcing

Tidak ada trade-off. Promote human dignity via capability enhancement = menciptakan cooperative advantage. Ini berbeda dari framing "CSR vs profit" yang sering zero-sum. Cooperative advantage adalah outcome natural dari genuine stakeholder capability enhancement.

Framework Implementasi

Step 1 — Identify Stakeholders dan Capabilities yang Relevant

Untuk setiap stakeholder group, identifikasi: apa capabilities yang mereka perlukan untuk functionings yang bernilai? Employees: skills, health, professional development. Suppliers: business skills, technology access, working capital. Customers: product literacy, financial capability. Communities: infrastructure, education, health.

Step 2 — Assess Current State vs. Potential

Apa gap antara current capabilities dan potential? Di mana perusahaan dapat contribute secara meaningful?

Step 3 — Design Capability Enhancement Programs

Specific programs yang address gaps:

  • Training programs untuk employees (bukan hanya job-specific tetapi career development).
  • Supplier development programs (training, certification, working capital).
  • Customer education programs (financial literacy, product usage, digital skills).
  • Community infrastructure investment.

Step 4 — Measure Actual Capability Improvements

Bukan inputs (money spent) tetapi outputs (capabilities gained). Metrics tangible: skills learned, businesses upgraded, income mobility achieved, health improvements, education completed.

Step 5 — Integrate dengan Business Strategy

Capability enhancement tidak side-program—ia integral dengan supply chain strategy, HR strategy, customer engagement strategy, community relations. Terintegrasi = cooperative advantage; terpisah = charity/compliance.

Kontribusi Teoretis

1. Mengintegrasikan Ethical + Strategic

Banyak literatur strategi treats ethics sebagai constraint (apa yang harus dihindari) atau external CSR (philanthropy). Artikel ini mengintegrasikan ethics ke strategi core.

2. Memperkenalkan Cooperative Advantage sebagai Kategori

Selain competitive advantage (Porter) dan resource-based advantage (Barney), cooperative advantage adalah kategori ketiga—value dari relationships. Konsisten dengan Dyer & Singh relational view.

3. Memberi Operational Framework

Capability approach Sen sering dikritik terlalu abstrak untuk management. Artikel ini operationalisasi ke management decisions.

Keterbatasan

  • **Konseptual, bukan empiris: belum ada measurement validated untuk capability enhancement. Perusahaan harus develop sendiri metrics.
  • **Complex implementation: identifying relevant capabilities per stakeholder group is resource-intensive.
  • **Long time horizon: capability enhancement takes years—returns on investment bisa tertunda—tidak cocok dengan quarterly earnings pressure.

Aplikasi ke Konteks Indonesia

Gojek Driver Ecosystem — Case Study

Pra-Gojek: driver ojek informal dengan limited capabilities—income unstable, tidak ada identitas formal, tidak ada insurance, tidak ada career path.

Post-Gojek: driver dengan formal identity (registered), income tracking, access to insurance, financial services (tabungan via GoPay), peer community, training programs (customer service, safety).

Evaluasi capability enhancement:

  • ✅ Digital literacy: drivers belajar menggunakan apps, manage ratings.
  • ✅ Financial literacy: tracking income, savings, credit history.
  • ✅ Health & safety: insurance coverage, safety training.
  • ⚠️ Independence: driver tergantung pada algorithm + platform policies.
  • ⚠️ Wage: meskipun income tracking ada, actual earnings masih volatile.
Gojek memang meningkatkan capability drivers dalam beberapa dimensi; tetapi juga menciptakan new dependencies. Debat akademis aktif apakah ini net capability enhancement atau sophisticated labor extraction.

BRI UMKM Ecosystem

BRI tidak hanya lending—invest dalam UMKM capability enhancement: financial literacy, business management training, digital tools (BRILink), market access. Clear net capability enhancement, cooperative advantage yang manifest dalam UMKM portfolio yang loyal dan NPL rendah.

Unilever Smallholder Programs

Sustainable sourcing yang tidak hanya "buy certified"—tetapi invest dalam smallholder training, certification achievement, farm management. Smallholders gain: higher yield, certified sustainable products (higher prices), better practices. Unilever gain: reliable supply chain, sustainability credentials. Classic cooperative advantage.

Pertanyaan Diskusi

Diskusi

Pilih perusahaan Indonesia yang Anda kenal baik. Apakah mereka secara genuine menghasilkan stakeholder capability enhancement (human dignity + cooperative advantage), atau hanya retoris tanpa substansi? Evaluasi dengan kerangka Westermann-Behaylo: identifikasi capabilities specific yang di-enhance, bagaimana diukur, dan apakah outcome valid untuk claim "human dignity" + "cooperative advantage".

Analisis Artikel 27 — Kumar & Pansari (2016)

Judul lengkap: Competitive Advantage through Engagement. Penulis: V. Kumar, Anita Pansari. Publikasi: Journal of Marketing Research, Vol. 53 No. 4 (August 2016), pp. 497–514. Tipe riset: empirical + conceptual dengan framework development dan case validation.

Catatan Sumber Primer

PDF artikel tidak disediakan. Analisis dari abstrak publik + literatur kanonik engagement (Reichheld 2003 Net Promoter Score; Harter et al. 2002 employee engagement meta-analysis; van Doorn et al. 2010 customer engagement; Brodie et al. 2011). Mahasiswa dianjurkan mencari PDF asli.

Pertanyaan Riset / Kontribusi

Apakah engagement—lebih dari sekedar satisfaction—dapat menjadi sumber sustainable competitive advantage? Jika ya, dimensi apa saja yang paling impactful, dan bagaimana measure + manage-nya?

Konseptualisasi: Engagement beyond Satisfaction

Satisfaction (Traditional)

Passive. "Saya puas dengan transaksi terakhir." Hygiene factor—diperlukan tetapi tidak distinguishing. Measurable post-transaction dengan surveys.

Engagement (Kumar & Pansari)

Active, multi-dimensional, ongoing. "Saya aktif terhubung dengan brand—emotionally, cognitively, behaviorally—beyond individual transactions." Manifests dalam behaviors: advocacy, feedback, co-creation, community participation, defensive behaviors saat brand under attack.

Framework — Four Pillars

Kumar & Pansari usulkan kerangka komprehensif dengan 4 pillars yang saling memperkuat:

Pillar 1 — Customer Engagement

Components:

  • Customer Purchases—transactional baseline.
  • Customer Referrals—bringing new customers (reducing CAC).
  • Customer Influence—word-of-mouth, social media impact, reviews.
  • Customer Knowledge Contribution—feedback, co-creation, product improvement.
Measurement: Customer Engagement Value (CEV) yang go beyond Customer Lifetime Value (CLV).

Pillar 2 — Employee Engagement

Components:

  • Cognitive engagement—focus, concentration, innovation contribution.
  • Emotional engagement—pride in company, caring about outcomes.
  • Behavioral engagement—discretionary effort, intent to stay.
Measurement: Gallup Q12 survey, Utrecht Work Engagement Scale, proprietary engagement indices.

Pillar 3 — Stakeholder Engagement

Components:

  • Supplier engagement—long-term partnerships, co-development.
  • Partner engagement—alliance relationships dengan trust.
  • Regulator engagement—proactive dialog, compliance culture.
  • NGO engagement—partnerships for complex social issues.

Pillar 4 — Societal Engagement

Components:

  • Community impact—local investment dan partnerships.
  • Environmental action—beyond compliance.
  • Policy engagement—contribution ke systemic issues.
  • Strategic CSR—terintegrasi ke core business (consistent dengan Porter-Kramer shared value).

Empirical Evidence (dari Paper + Meta-literatur)

Penelitian yang Kumar & Pansari referensikan dan contribute:

Customer Engagement Impact

Studies menunjukkan: customers highly engaged menghasilkan 23% higher share-of-wallet, 43% more likely to refer, and 2x likely to defend brand during PR crises (Gallup).

Employee Engagement Impact

Gallup meta-analysis (Harter et al. 2002): quartile top companies berdasarkan employee engagement menunjukkan:

  • 21% higher productivity.
  • 22% higher profitability.
  • 10% higher customer ratings.
  • 37% lower absenteeism.

Integrated Effect

Kumar & Pansari argue: impact bukan additive tetapi multiplicative. Engaged employees serve engaged customers better, yang engage stakeholders lebih dalam, yang strengthen societal engagement, yang attract engaged employees—virtuous cycle.

Managerial Implications

1. Measure All Four Pillars Regularly

Banyak perusahaan hanya measure customer satisfaction atau employee satisfaction—tidak engagement, tidak all four pillars. Kumar & Pansari recommend quarterly tracking.

2. Engagement Dashboards

Include engagement metrics di senior management dashboard—bukan hanya finansial. CEOs harus bertanggung jawab atas engagement sebagai key outcome.

3. Investment dalam Engagement Drivers

Drivers termasuk: purpose-driven culture, quality products, fair compensation, community investment, transparent communication, stakeholder dialog. Semua ini investment jangka panjang dengan returns yang compound.

4. Engagement sebagai Competitive Moat

Engagement ecosystem sulit direplikasi: butuh tahun untuk build, bergantung pada trust, embedded dalam culture. Kompetitor yang hanya copy products atau processes tanpa build engagement—akan gagal match performance.

Kontribusi Teoretis

  • Mengintegrasikan beberapa literatur yang sebelumnya terpisah (customer engagement, employee engagement, stakeholder theory, CSR).
  • Memberi kerangka operasional untuk measurement + management.
  • Bukti empiris solid untuk klaim bahwa engagement → performance.

Keterbatasan

  • **Measurement complexity: 4 pillars memerlukan multiple measurement systems yang dapat overwhelm smaller organizations.
  • **Attribution: sulit memisahkan kontribusi 4 pillars terhadap kinerja (mungkin overlapping atau interdependent).
  • **Context dependency: optimal mix of pillars mungkin bergantung industri, ukuran, maturity perusahaan.

Aplikasi ke Indonesia

BCA — Customer + Employee Engagement yang Kuat

BCA consistently peringkat top di customer satisfaction surveys di Indonesia. NPS yang kuat. Employee engagement melalui BDP (Banker Development Program), SMART culture, long tenure manajemen. 4 pillars relatif strong. Cooperative advantage yang manifest dalam dominant market position di CASA.

Gojek / GoTo — Multi-Side Engagement

Platform business yang by design membutuhkan engagement multi-side: driver engagement (earning opportunity, community), consumer engagement (loyalty, advocacy), merchant engagement (partnership, tools), societal engagement (CSR, regulatory dialog). 4 pillars kritikal untuk success.

BUMN yang Perlu Tingkatkan Engagement

Banyak BUMN Indonesia (PLN, Pertamina, Garuda) secara historis fokus pada operational compliance, bukan engagement. Recent improvements via AKHLAK values, customer experience programs, employee engagement surveys—tetapi masih banyak gap dibanding private sector leaders.

Pertanyaan Diskusi

Diskusi

Desain Engagement Dashboard untuk sebuah perusahaan Indonesia yang Anda pilih. Minimum 3 KPI per pillar (total 12+). Identifikasi: (a) measurement approach, (b) target/benchmark, (c) links ke business outcomes. Pertahankan setiap pilihan dengan argumen strategis.

④ Indonesian Company Examples · Minggu 13

Gojek Driver Ecosystem — Stakeholder Capability Enhancement

Jangkar konsep: stakeholder capability enhancement (Westermann-Behaylo et al. 2016); cooperative advantage dari relational investment; 4 pillars of engagement (Kumar-Pansari) di platform business; debat apakah gig economy enhances atau extracts value dari drivers.

Gojek adalah case study paling fundamental untuk diskusi stakeholder capability enhancement di Indonesia. Sebelum Gojek (2010), driver ojek adalah most informal economic actors—income unstable, tidak ada formal identitas, tidak ada safety nets. Gojek menciptakan infrastructure yang secara significantly mengubah capabilities ini—sekaligus menciptakan new dependencies yang debated di literatur.

Gojek Driver Ecosystem — Profile

Part of GoTo · IDX: GOTO
MillionsDriver PartnersGoTo AR 2023, Platform Statistics
DigitizedInformal Ojek EconomyPre-Gojek 2010 vs. current state
Cross-verticalDrivers work multiple GoTo servicesPlatform business model

Capability Enhancement — Dimensi yang Nyata

1. Formal Economic Identity

Pra-Gojek: driver ojek tidak memiliki formal identity—tidak terdaftar, tidak ada track record, tidak ada history transaksi.

Post-Gojek: driver memiliki digital identity di platform (GoPartner), dokumen KTP verified, rating system yang tracks performance over time, history of earnings. Ini fundamental capability enhancement—prerequisite untuk akses ke formal financial services.

2. Income Tracking & Financial Literacy

Pra-Gojek: cash-based, no tracking, mudah hilang atau dicuri. Planning finansial minimal.

Post-Gojek: real-time earnings tracking di app, GoPay wallet, transaction history. Drivers can analyze earnings patterns, plan. Beberapa partner dengan BRI (GoPay-BRI co-branded) untuk formal banking access. Financial literacy capability meningkat.

3. Access to Insurance & Safety Nets

Pra-Gojek: tidak ada insurance. Kecelakaan = bankruptcy untuk driver families.

Post-Gojek: driver insurance disediakan platform (accident coverage). Beberapa programs untuk health dan long-term safety nets. Belum sempurna tetapi improvement substantial.

4. Skills Development

Platform menyediakan training:

  • Customer service skills (handling complaints, professionalism).
  • Safety training (defensive riding, traffic awareness).
  • Platform literacy (app usage, GPS optimization).
  • Financial skills via GoPay + partnerships.
Drivers gain employability skills yang transferable ke pekerjaan lain jika leave platform.

5. Peer Community & Collective Voice

Driver communities terbentuk (KOMPAG, GARDA, various regional groups). Formal organizations untuk advocacy, peer support, knowledge sharing. Ini capability collective yang tidak ada pre-Gojek.

6. Career Mobility

Beberapa driver pindah ke roles lain di ekosistem: GoSend courier, GoMart, GoCar; beberapa menjadi entrepreneurial seperti buy/sell vehicles, open warung. Platform sebagai stepping stone untuk mobility ke pekerjaan lebih formal.

Cooperative Advantage untuk Gojek/GoTo

Dari perspektif Gojek, investment dalam capability enhancement menghasilkan:

1. Reliable Driver Pool

Drivers yang trained + committed menyediakan service quality yang lebih baik dari informal alternative. Competitor yang hanya "menyuruh" driver tanpa capability enhancement akan memiliki quality gaps.

2. Brand Authority Social

"Gojek helps drivers" adalah narrative yang secara konsisten diangkat di media Indonesia. Ini brand authority yang sulit direplikasi Grab (perceived as foreign) atau new entrant.

3. Regulatory License to Operate

Pemerintah Indonesia secara implicit supports Gojek karena dianggap improving livelihoods. Jika regulatory pressure increase, Gojek memiliki lebih banyak social capital untuk navigate.

4. Supply-Side Network Effect

Driver yang engaged + capability-enhanced cenderung stay longer. Low driver churn berarti lebih stable service supply, yang drive consumer satisfaction, yang drive growth.

4 Pillars Engagement Analysis (Kumar-Pansari)

Customer Engagement

GoTo membangun consumer engagement via app experience, loyalty programs (GoPoints), campaigns. Score relatif tinggi—aplikasi sering dibuka, consumers actively use multiple services cross-vertically.

Employee Engagement

Drivers dapat dianggap sebagai quasi-employees (meskipun legally contractors). Engagement programs berjalan tetapi debate apakah cukup given flexible labor model. Karyawan formal (tech engineers, ops) memiliki engagement yang standar di industri tech.

Stakeholder Engagement

Partnerships dengan banks (untuk financial services), regulators (OJK, Kemenhub), NGOs untuk driver welfare issues. Ini dimensi yang aktif dikelola.

Societal Engagement

CSR programs (disaster response, community grants), public policy engagement (sometimes controversial around gig economy rules), environmental initiatives (EV pilot programs).

Debat: Enhancement vs. Extraction

Literatur gig economy (Rosenblat 2018; Muldoon 2022; studi Indonesia oleh peneliti seperti LPEM FEB UI) raise concerns:

Pro-Enhancement Argument

  • Drivers memiliki flexibility yang tidak dimiliki employees traditional.
  • Formal identity + financial access adalah real capability gain.
  • Entry to economic activity yang sebelumnya tidak ada.

Pro-Extraction Argument

  • Algorithmic management = de-facto control tanpa formal employer obligations.
  • Take-rate yang tinggi (platform ambil significant cut).
  • Benefits limited dibanding formal employees (no pension, limited health insurance).
  • Dependency pada platform—driver tidak memiliki leverage.

Balanced Assessment

Gojek driver ecosystem net positive capability enhancement untuk most drivers—especially given alternative adalah informal ojek yang lebih vulnerable. Namun enhancement juga menciptakan new types of dependencies. Academic dan policy debate akan continue.

Untuk strategic management students: ini case yang rich untuk menganalisis kompleksitas stakeholder capability enhancement dalam konteks platform business.

Sidebar 1 — Tokopedia Seller Engagement

Jangkar konsep: supplier/partner engagement (Kumar-Pansari pillar 3); capability enhancement untuk UMKM seller; cooperative advantage via seller community.

Tokopedia (bagian dari GoTo) membangun platform e-commerce melalui cooperative advantage dengan jutaan sellers—kebanyakan UMKM Indonesia. Berbeda dari Amazon yang lebih vertical (Amazon sebagai retailer sendiri), Tokopedia primarily sebagai marketplace yang empowers seller ekosistem.

Capability Enhancement untuk Sellers

1. Access to Market

Pra-Tokopedia: UMKM lokal limited ke geographic radius. Post-Tokopedia: seller di Aceh dapat menjual ke konsumen di Papua. Fundamental market access capability enhancement.

2. Digital Skills Training

Kelas Seller, Seller Center educational content, Tokopedia Digital Assistant, onboarding support. Sellers gain digital skills yang transferable—ecommerce literacy, online marketing, customer service, digital photography.

3. Business Management Tools

Dashboard analytics, inventory management, sales reporting, customer insights. Sellers belajar manage business dengan data—capability yang previously required expensive tools.

4. Financial Access

Working capital loans via Tokopedia Modal Toko, partnerships dengan financial institutions. UMKM sellers gain access ke formal credit yang sebelumnya sulit diperoleh.

5. Community & Peer Support

Seller community yang aktif (forum, WhatsApp groups, events). Sellers saling membantu—knowledge sharing, best practices, collective problem solving.

Cooperative Advantage untuk Tokopedia

  • **Marketplace liquidity: jutaan sellers → product variety → consumer attraction.
  • **Network effect: more sellers → more consumers → attract more sellers.
  • **Brand positioning: "Tokopedia empowers UMKM" adalah narrative resonan di Indonesia.

Sidebar 2 — BCA Customer Loyalty

Jangkar konsep: customer engagement beyond satisfaction (Kumar-Pansari); long-term relational capital sebagai VRIN; brand community effects.

BCA (Minggu 2, 4 dibahas sebelumnya) adalah contoh paling prominent dari customer engagement di perbankan Indonesia. Dengan CASA ratio tertinggi di Indonesia (~80%), BCA membuktikan bahwa customers tidak hanya puas—mereka engaged dalam way yang sulit direplikasi kompetitor.

BCA — Customer Engagement Signals

IDX: BBCA
~80%CASA Ratio (industry-leading)BCA AR 2023
~29 jutaCustomer AccountsBCA AR 2023
DecadesLong-term Customer RelationshipsBCA corporate history

Engagement Signals (Beyond Satisfaction)

1. Deposit Behavior (Engagement via Trust)

CASA ratio 80% berarti customers menjaga dana di BCA bukan untuk transaksi temporary tetapi sebagai primary banking relationship. Ini trust-level yang tinggi—customers engage dengan BCA sebagai financial hub.

2. Cross-Product Adoption

Customers BCA yang memiliki tabungan cenderung juga memiliki credit card, mobile banking, investasi products (WeLma), kredit (KPR, KTA). Multi-product adoption adalah engagement signal—relationship deepens beyond single transaksi.

3. Word-of-Mouth & Advocacy

Kustomer BCA sering merekomendasikan ke keluarga. BCA sebagai "default bank" untuk keluarga-keluarga terjadi multi-generational. Organic customer acquisition significant.

4. Defensive Behavior

Saat ada krisis (krisis 1998, tech issues, negative news), customers BCA cenderung memberi benefit of doubt—tidak panic withdraw seperti yang dialami banks lain. Ini emotional engagement yang built over decades.

5. Feedback & Co-Creation

BCA actively collects feedback via surveys, branch interactions, app reviews. Features baru (OneKlik, QRIS integration) sering originated dari customer feedback. Customers contribute ke product development.

Employee Engagement (Pillar 2)

BCA memiliki culture yang distinctive (SMART values—Solutions, Mission, Attitude, Respect, Teamwork). Employee engagement programs:

  • Banker Development Program (BDP)—prestige program yang attract top talent.
  • Tenure management yang predictable (Jahja Setiaatmadja sebagai presdir sejak 2011).
  • Internal promotion culture.
  • SMART values yang lived (not just posters).

Employee engagement yang tinggi → customer engagement yang tinggi—virtuous cycle dalam Kumar-Pansari framework.

Stakeholder & Societal Engagement

Stakeholder Engagement

  • OJK regulatory dialog (BCA sebagai SIFI—systemically important financial institution).
  • Djarum family (major shareholder) sebagai long-term stakeholder, bukan short-term trader.
  • Partnerships dengan ribuan merchants untuk payment infrastructure.

Societal Engagement

  • Bakti BCA (CSR foundation) focus pada education, entrepreneurship, culture.
  • Long-term partnerships dengan top universities (Bina Nusantara, beberapa beasiswa programs).
  • Support untuk UMKM community initiatives.

Kontras Tiga Flagship Minggu 13

PerusahaanFocus EngagementCapability Enhancement
Gojek driversSupplier (driver) sideFormal identity, digital literacy, financial access
Tokopedia sellersSupplier (seller) sideMarket access, digital skills, business management tools
BCA customersCustomer sideFinancial services, trust, long-term relationships

Semua tiga menunjukkan cooperative advantage via stakeholder engagement—bukan hanya competitive advantage via products. Durability dari advantage ini jauh lebih tinggi dari product differentiation yang dapat disalin.

Pelajaran Strategis Umum

  1. Engagement butuh waktu. BCA membangun customer engagement selama 50+ tahun; Gojek drivers ecosystem membangun selama 15 tahun. Tidak ada shortcut.
  2. Engagement butuh investment. Training programs, technology platforms, community building—semua memerlukan capital allocation yang konsisten.
  3. Engagement memerlukan leadership commitment. Jika leadership tidak percaya pada relational capital, engagement akan limited ke marketing programs superficial.
  4. Engagement = cooperative advantage = moat. Pelajaran utama: in age of rapid technology change, relational capital adalah moat yang paling durable.

Topik dipilih secara sengaja sebagai capstone: dua konsep yang mengintegrasikan banyak tema yang dipelajari selama 13 minggu—hypercompetition (lingkungan kompetisi yang paling intens) dan strategic leadership (kapabilitas puncak yang dituntut untuk navigasi lingkungan itu).

Catatan Mapping: Silabus tidak menugaskan TPGS chapter untuk minggu ini. Kami anchor pada Henry Bab 3 (competitive dynamics) dan Bab 11 (organisational change & leadership) plus dua artikel penelitian yang menjadi drivers tematik.

Review konsep external environment dari Minggu 3 dengan fokus pada dynamic competitive environments—hypercompetition, temporary advantages, competitive interactions.

"Navigating in a Hypercompetitive Environment: The Roles of Action Aggressiveness and TMT Integration." Empiris—bagaimana top management team (TMT) integration + action aggressiveness mempengaruhi kinerja di lingkungan hypercompetitive. PDF tidak disediakan.

"Strategic Leadership for Exploration and Exploitation: The Moderating Role of Environmental Dynamism." Minggu 14 juga waktu untuk review 14 minggu secara keseluruhan sebagai persiapan UAS. Gunakan Visual Companion + Master Summary untuk mengintegrasikan pembelajaran.

Enam Konsep Inti — Minggu 14

1. Hypercompetition (D'Aveni 1994)

Richard D'Aveni dalam Hypercompetition (1994) mendefinisikan hypercompetition sebagai environment di mana:

  • Competitive advantages temporary—terkikis cepat.
  • Competitive interactions aggressive, frequent, unpredictable.
  • Traditional sources of sustainable advantage (economies of scale, brand, regulasi) insufficient.
Industri yang paling hypercompetitive: tech platforms, media digital, fintech, e-commerce. Key insight: dalam hypercompetition, strategi shift dari "defend existing advantage" ke "continuously create new temporary advantages".

2. Action Aggressiveness

Frekuensi dan intensitas competitive actions (price changes, product launches, advertising campaigns, strategic alliances). Chen, Lin & Michel (2010) menunjukkan: di hypercompetitive environments, firms dengan higher action aggressiveness mencapai better performance—asalkan didukung TMT integration yang baik. Without TMT integration, aggressive actions become uncoordinated dan destructive.

3. Upper Echelons Theory (Hambrick & Mason 1984)

Organizational outcomes—strategic choices, performance—adalah reflection dari characteristics top management team (TMT): age, tenure, functional background, education, cognitive base. TMT sebagai strategic actor, bukan hanya "the executives". Implikasi: studying leadership characteristics membantu predicting organizational behavior.

4. TMT Integration (Chen, Lin & Michel 2010)

Seberapa baik top management team berfungsi sebagai integrated unit—shared vision, communication quality, decision-making coordination, collaborative behavior. TMT integration memoderasi relationship antara action aggressiveness dan performance. Di hypercompetitive environments, TMT yang integrated dapat eksekusi aggressive actions effectively; TMT yang fragmented justru menghasilkan chaos.

5. Exploration vs. Exploitation (March 1991)

James March (1991) mengidentifikasi dua aktivitas fundamentally different:

  • Exploration: search, variation, experimentation, discovery of new opportunities. Future-oriented, uncertain returns.
  • Exploitation: refinement, efficiency, execution, optimization of current opportunities. Present-oriented, certain returns.
Tension: resources allocated to one reduce resources for the other. Organizational ambidexterity—kemampuan melakukan keduanya simultaneously—adalah capability yang sangat sulit.

6. Ambidextrous Leadership (Jansen, Vera & Crossan 2009)

Transformational leadership (vision, inspiration, intellectual stimulation) mendukung exploration. Transactional leadership (clear goals, contingent rewards, management-by-exception) mendukung exploitation. Ambidextrous leaders dapat switch antara keduanya—atau different leaders dalam TMT exhibit different styles. Dimoderasi oleh environmental dynamism: di dynamic environments, exploration lebih valued; di stable environments, exploitation lebih cukup.

Minggu 14 dalam Peta Mata Kuliah (Capstone)

Minggu 14 adalah capstone—mengintegrasikan banyak tema dari 13 minggu sebelumnya. Lihat dan pelajari matriks di bawah sebagai peta jalan untuk UAS preparation.

MingguBagaimana Minggu 14 Mengintegrasikan
1Definisi strategi—dalam hypercompetition, strategi = continuous adaptation
2Leadership penting di semua 5 tahap proses; Minggu 14 memperdalam strategic leadership
3Mason 2007 complexity—hypercompetition adalah complexity extreme
4Dynamic capabilities Teece = exploration capability di Jansen framework
5–6Temporary advantage = strategi generik + supplementing moves yang terus bergerak
7Tailoring ke industry lifecycle: mature → hypercompetition (shakeout) transitions
8International hypercompetition: GoTo vs. Grab (regional scale)
9Diversifikasi sebagai hedge against hypercompetition di single industry
10ESG sebagai differentiator ketika product differentiation sulit dipertahankan
11Eksekusi dan culture—ambidextrous leaders build culture untuk exploration+exploitation
12Business model innovation sebagai mechanism creating temporary advantages
13Stakeholder engagement = cooperative advantage yang sulit direplikasi di hypercompetition

Empat Hubungan Konseptual Kunci (Capstone-Level)

  1. **Hypercompetition ↔ Temporary Advantage. Traditional strategic management (Porter Five Forces, RBV) mengasumsikan sustainable advantage. Hypercompetition framework mengingatkan: mungkin yang realistic adalah sequence of temporary advantages. Ini menuntut dynamic capabilities (Minggu 4) dan continuous business model innovation (Minggu 12).
  2. **TMT Integration ↔ Execution. Kumar-Pansari engagement (Minggu 13) dan Kaplan-Norton execution (Minggu 11) konvergen pada pentingnya senior leadership alignment. Chen, Lin & Michel (2010) menambahkan: integration adalah prasyarat effective aggressive action.
  3. **Exploration ↔ Innovation Capability. Exploration March (1991) = business model innovation (Minggu 12) + dynamic capabilities (Minggu 4) + culture of experimentation (Mason 2007 learning organization). Perusahaan yang low exploration accumulate technical debt dan menjadi rigid.
  4. **Leadership Style ↔ Environment. Jansen et al. (2009): tidak ada single best leadership style. Di dynamic environments, transformational (exploration-enabling) lebih valuable; di stable environments, transactional (exploitation-enabling) cukup. Contextual leadership.

Fokus Diskusi — Minggu 14 & UAS Preparation

Minggu 14 adalah last tatap-muka sebelum UAS. Empat tingkat diskusi (tingkat kompleksitas capstone):

Tingkat 1 — Fokus Minggu Ini

  1. **Hypercompetition di Indonesia. Tiga industri Indonesia yang paling hypercompetitive: ride-hailing (GoTo vs Grab vs ShopeeFood), e-commerce (Tokopedia vs Shopee vs Lazada), fintech lending. Apakah D'Aveni framework relevan untuk Indonesia? Dynamic apa yang unik?
  2. **Strategic leadership Indonesia. Pilih dua pemimpin perusahaan Indonesia yang kontras—satu yang lebih transformational (vision-driven, bold moves), satu yang lebih transactional (execution-focused, process). Analisis dengan kerangka Jansen et al.
  3. **TMT integration case study. Identifikasi satu perusahaan Indonesia yang gagal karena TMT fragmentation atau konflik. Apa pelajaran strategis?
  4. **Ambidextrous leadership. Mungkinkah satu pemimpin benar-benar ambidextrous? Atau harus ambidexterity di level TMT (different leaders dengan different strengths)?

Tingkat 2 — Integrasi 14 Minggu

  1. **Sintesis kerangka strategis. Buatlah diagram yang mengintegrasikan: Porter Five Forces + VRIN + Generic Strategies + Supplementing + Tailoring + International + Diversification + CSR + Execution + Business Model Innovation + Stakeholder + Hypercompetition. Mana saling reinforce, mana saling tension?
  2. **Indonesia as context. Institutional voids, emerging market dinamika, regulasi yang evolving, budaya. Bagaimana konteks ini mengubah applicability kerangka strategic management barat?

Tingkat 3 — UAS-Style Questions (Case Analysis)

  1. **Multi-lens analysis. Pilih satu perusahaan Indonesia (BCA, GoTo, Unilever, Astra—atau lain). Analisis menggunakan minimum 5 kerangka berbeda dari 14 minggu. Sintesis insights.
  2. **Strategic recommendation. Sebagai CEO, rekomendasi strategis apa yang akan Anda buat untuk sebuah perusahaan Indonesia yang menghadapi hypercompetition? Pertahankan dengan multi-framework analysis.

Tingkat 4 — Kritis dan Reflektif

  1. **Limitations of Western frameworks. Kerangka strategi mana yang paling berguna untuk Indonesia? Yang kurang? Apa yang perlu diadaptasi?
  2. **Future of strategic management. Dengan AI, climate change, geopolitical tension—bagaimana strategic management akan berevolusi? Prediksi untuk Indonesia dalam 10 tahun ke depan.

Pemeriksa Konsep

Pemeriksa Konsep · Capstone Integration

K1. Hypercompetition D'Aveni: apakah ini fundamental different dari "competitive rivalry" Porter Five Forces? Atau continuum? Pertahankan dengan contoh Indonesia.

K2. Chen, Lin & Michel: action aggressiveness × TMT integration = performance. Mana lebih penting di Indonesia—aggressive action atau TMT integration? Mengapa?

K3. Jansen et al.: transformational untuk exploration, transactional untuk exploitation. Berikan contoh dua CEO Indonesia yang exemplify masing-masing style. Yang mana outperform long-term?

K4. March's exploration-exploitation tradeoff: apakah tradeoff ini fundamental (mutually exclusive), atau dapat di-transcend dengan organizational design yang tepat (ambidextrous organization)?

K5. Capstone question: Pilih satu perusahaan Indonesia. Analisis: (a) posisi competitive, (b) sumber keunggulan, (c) hypercompetitive threats, (d) TMT characteristics, (e) leadership style, (f) strategic recommendation. Gunakan minimum 5 kerangka dari 14 minggu.

② Main Summary / Ebook · Minggu 14

Ikhtisar Minggu 14 (Capstone)

Referensi: Henry Ch.3 (External Environment: Hypercompetition) · Henry Ch.11 (Strategic Leadership & Change) · Art.28 Chen, Lin & Michel (2010) · Art.29 Jansen, Vera & Crossan (2009)

Minggu 14 adalah capstone dari mata kuliah Manajemen Strategik Kontemporer. Dua topik yang dipilih untuk minggu final dengan sengaja:

In hypercompetitive environments, the rules of strategy change: sustainable competitive advantage becomes elusive, and the capability to continuously create and destroy advantages—led by integrated top management teams—becomes the source of superior performance. Adaptasi dari Chen, Lin & Michel — Organization Science (2010)

Tema 1 — Hypercompetition

Richard D'Aveni (1994) dalam Hypercompetition menantang premise tradisional strategi: sustainable competitive advantage. Di industri modern yang paling dinamis, advantages adalah temporary—competitor respond cepat, technology bergeser, consumer preferences berubah. Perusahaan yang berhasil di hypercompetition bukan yang build unassailable fortresses tetapi yang continuously create sequences of temporary advantages.

Chen, Lin & Michel (2010) memperdalam dengan studi empiris: action aggressiveness (frequency + intensity competitive moves) meningkatkan kinerja di hypercompetitive environments, tetapi hanya jika didukung TMT integration yang strong. Tanpa TMT integration, aggressive actions become uncoordinated dan destructive.

Tema 2 — Strategic Leadership

Upper echelons theory (Hambrick & Mason 1984): organizational outcomes reflect TMT characteristics. Strategic leadership bukan hanya soft skill—ia fundamental driver of organizational behavior dan performance.

Jansen, Vera & Crossan (2009) mengintegrasikan strategic leadership dengan tension exploration-exploitation (March 1991):

  • Transformational leadership (vision, intellectual stimulation, inspirational motivation) mendukung exploration—innovation, experimentation, new capabilities.
  • Transactional leadership (clear goals, contingent rewards, management-by-exception) mendukung exploitation—efficiency, execution, refinement of existing capabilities.

Ambidextrous leadership—kemampuan untuk enable keduanya—adalah capability puncak yang sangat sulit achieve tetapi critical di dynamic environments.

Mengapa Capstone

Minggu 14 mengintegrasikan:

  • Minggu 3 (external environment): hypercompetition adalah extreme case.
  • Minggu 4 (VRIN + dynamic capabilities): temporary advantages menuntut dynamic capabilities.
  • Minggu 5-7 (strategy formulation): rapid strategy formulation di hypercompetition.
  • Minggu 11 (execution): TMT integration = prerequisite for effective execution.
  • Minggu 12 (business model innovation): mechanism untuk create new temporary advantages.
  • Minggu 13 (stakeholder engagement): moderator of hypercompetition impact.

Untuk mahasiswa Magister Akuntansi yang akan menjadi senior professionals atau executives—minggu ini adalah preparation untuk realitas strategic management di era digital: continuous adaptation under uncertainty.

Hypercompetition Framework (D'Aveni 1994)

Richard D'Aveni dalam Hypercompetition: Managing the Dynamics of Strategic Maneuvering (1994) menawarkan perspektif yang menantang literatur strategic management dominan.

Premise: Sustainable Advantage is an Illusion

Tradisi Porter dan Barney mengasumsikan perusahaan dapat membangun sustainable competitive advantage melalui industry positioning atau VRIN resources. D'Aveni menantang:

The only advantage that is truly sustainable is the ability to create a series of temporary advantages faster than competitors can imitate them. Richard D'Aveni — Hypercompetition (1994)

Empat Arena Competitive Dynamics

D'Aveni identifikasi empat arena di mana competitive interactions terjadi:

1. Cost & Quality Arena

Kompetisi tradisional—Porter's generic strategies. Incumbents dapat membangun scale advantages, quality reputations. Namun di hypercompetition: competitor dengan quick imitation dapat erode advantages rapidly.

2. Timing & Know-How Arena

First-mover advantages, knowledge leadership. Di hypercompetition: first-movers face risk of "first-mover disadvantage"—educating market yang kemudian dimasuki fast followers yang leverage insights.

3. Strongholds Arena

Building defensive positions via economies of scale, deep pockets, geographic dominance. Di hypercompetition: deep pockets dapat drain jika prolonged war; geographic strongholds tersinggung oleh digital disruption.

4. Deep Pockets Arena

Financial staying power. Di hypercompetition: capital markets reward growth + paths to profitability—deep pockets tanpa strategic direction tidak sufficient.

Implikasi untuk Strategic Management

1. Shift dari "Defend" ke "Attack"

Traditional: build competitive advantage, defend it. Hypercompetition: continuously create new advantages, even if existing ones still viable. "Continuous disruption of own advantages" sebelum competitor.

2. Accept Temporary Advantages as Norm

Instead of searching for "unassailable" positions, accept that advantages are temporary. Build capability untuk create-exploit-abandon cycles faster than competitors.

3. Aggressive Action as Default

In stable environments, passive/reactive strategies viable. In hypercompetition, passive = slow death. Aggressive action—price moves, product launches, strategic alliances, M&A—becomes the norm.

Industri yang Paling Hypercompetitive

  • Tech platforms: advantages eroded quickly by new entrants or established players pivoting.
  • Fintech: regulasi evolving, new entrants constant, customer loyalty low.
  • E-commerce: platform consolidation + shakeout + live commerce disruption.
  • Media digital: advertising revenue volatile, consumer attention fragmented.
  • Smartphone manufacturing: rapid technology cycles, commoditization risk.

Industri yang Relatif Bukan Hypercompetitive

  • Utilities (PLN): regulated monopoly/oligopoly.
  • Heavy infrastructure: capital intensity + long cycles.
  • Consumer staples (Indofood): moderate change, strong brand moats.
  • Perbankan konsumer Indonesia (4 bank besar): regulated, moderate digital disruption (tapi meningkat).

Chen, Lin & Michel (2010) — Empirical Validation

Penelitian empiris mereka menunjukkan:

Finding 1 — Action Aggressiveness Matters di Hypercompetition

Firms dengan higher action aggressiveness (more frequent + intense competitive moves) achieve better performance in hypercompetitive environments. Passive firms mengalami decline.

Finding 2 — TMT Integration as Moderator

Aggressive actions without TMT integration = chaos. Actions uncoordinated, conflicting signals, execution failures. TMT integration = prerequisite for harnessing aggressive action into coherent strategic advantage.

Finding 3 — Context Specificity

Action aggressiveness beneficial terutama di hypercompetitive; di stable environments, over-aggressive actions dapat menjadi costly waste.

Kritik terhadap Hypercompetition Framework

  • Overstatement: tidak semua industri adalah hypercompetitive; banyak traditional industries yang tetap stable.
  • Selection bias: cases yang dianalisis D'Aveni adalah industri tech + consumer electronics—tidak generalize untuk semua.
  • Burnout risk: continuous aggressive action dapat exhaust organization—sustainability questioned.
  • Self-fulfilling prophecy: jika semua perusahaan mengadopsi hypercompetition mindset, industri menjadi lebih destructive untuk semua.

Keseimbangan Pragmatis

Most realistic pandangan: spectrum of competitive intensity. Some industries (perbankan konsumer, semen, consumer staples) mendekati stable; some (tech platforms, fintech) mendekati hypercompetitive. Strategic management yang canggih: diagnose where industry is, calibrate strategy accordingly.

Upper Echelons Theory (Hambrick & Mason 1984)

Donald Hambrick & Phyllis Mason dalam artikel seminal Academy of Management Review (1984) mengusulkan upper echelons theory: organizations are a reflection of their top managers.

Inti Argumen

Strategic decisions di organisasi kompleks sering complicated—involving ambiguity, uncertainty, multiple interpretations. Dalam kondisi ini, cognitive base dari decision-makers (top management team) menjadi critical. Manager membawa:

Demographic Characteristics

  • Age: older managers cenderung risk-averse.
  • Tenure: longer tenure cenderung commit ke status quo.
  • Functional background: finance-heavy TMT cenderung defensive, marketing-heavy cenderung expansive.
  • Education: formal education levels correlate dengan strategic choices.
  • Socioeconomic background: affect risk tolerance, stakeholder orientation.

Psychological Characteristics

  • Cognitive base: mental models dari past experiences.
  • Values: what managers consider important (profit, growth, social impact).
  • Risk tolerance: willingness to take bold actions.

Implikasi

Organizational outcomes—strategy choices, innovation rate, financial performance, response to crisis—reflect TMT characteristics. Untuk understand organization, study its TMT.

Research Evidence

Decades of research menguji upper echelons:

  • TMT functional diversity → strategic diversity dan innovation.
  • TMT tenure homogeneity → strategic persistence (resistance to change).
  • TMT age heterogeneity → better adaptation to dynamic environments.
  • TMT education → strategic sophistication + scanning behavior.

TMT Integration (Chen, Lin & Michel 2010)

Selain characteristics, TMT integration—bagaimana TMT berfungsi sebagai unit—matters significantly.

Dimensions of TMT Integration

  • Shared vision: alignment pada strategic direction.
  • Communication quality: open dialogue, information sharing.
  • Decision-making coordination: integrated decisions, not siloed.
  • Collaborative behavior: mutual support, constructive conflict.
  • Role clarity: understanding each other's responsibilities.

Why TMT Integration Matters in Hypercompetition

Di hypercompetitive environments yang memerlukan aggressive action:

  • Speed: integrated TMT dapat decide + execute cepat.
  • Coherence: aggressive actions consistent, tidak contradict.
  • Resilience: ketika actions fail (inevitable in hypercompetition), integrated TMT recover together.
  • Learning: integrated TMT extract lessons dari outcomes, improve future decisions.
TMT yang fragmented menghasilkan:
  • Slow decisions (political conflicts).
  • Contradictory signals to organization.
  • Execution failures (different TMT members pulling different directions).
  • Blame culture when actions fail.

Aplikasi ke Indonesia

BCA — High TMT Integration

Jahja Setiaatmadja sebagai Presdir sejak 2011—kontinuitas kepemimpinan yang langka. TMT BCA consistently integrated via shared SMART values, internal promotion culture (executives grew together), predictable decision processes. Hasil: execution yang konsisten dan strong performance selama 2 decades.

Garuda Indonesia — Low TMT Integration (Historis)

Pre-2020 Garuda: multiple CEO changes, politik yang kompleks (BUMN dengan pressure politis), conflicting priorities. TMT fragmented antara commercial vs. government mandate perspectives. Contributing factor untuk crisis yang accumulated.

GoTo — TMT Integration Challenge Post-Merger

Merger Gojek + Tokopedia (2021) menciptakan TMT integration challenge—different corporate cultures (Gojek as technical ops, Tokopedia as marketplace), different decision processes, different leadership styles. Post-merger integration journey masih berjalan. Kinerja post-pivot yang solid menunjukkan TMT integration sedang membaik.

Implikasi untuk Strategic Management

1. Hire, Develop, Manage TMT Carefully

TMT composition = strategic decision. Siapa yang ada di TMT (background, values, styles) akan shape strategic behavior organization for years to come.

2. Build TMT Integration Deliberately

Integration tidak spontan. Invest dalam: TMT retreats, communication norms, shared planning processes, conflict resolution mechanisms.

3. Diversity Plus Integration

TMT yang homogeneous dan integrated dapat groupthink. TMT yang diverse tetapi fragmented chaos. Sweet spot: diverse perspectives plus integrated functioning. Hardest untuk achieve—membutuhkan intentional leadership.

4. Succession Planning as Strategic Priority

TMT transitions adalah moments of vulnerability. Good strategic management include rigorous succession planning untuk maintain integration across leadership changes.

Exploration-Exploitation Tension (March 1991)

James March dalam artikel klasik Organization Science (1991) mengidentifikasi tension fundamental dalam organizational learning:

Exploration

Search, variation, experimentation, discovery. Activities yang explore new possibilities, develop new capabilities, create future options. Karakteristik: uncertain returns, long time horizons, high variance outcomes. Example: R&D, new market entry, disruptive technology development.

Exploitation

Refinement, efficiency, execution, selection of known alternatives. Activities yang exploit existing capabilities for current returns. Karakteristik: certain returns, short time horizons, low variance outcomes. Example: operational improvements, cost reduction, scaling proven products.

Tension

Organizations allocate finite resources (capital, talent, management attention). Resources untuk exploration berkurang exploitation. Resources untuk exploitation berkurang exploration. Tradeoff.

The basic problem confronting an organization is to engage in sufficient exploitation to ensure its current viability and, at the same time, devote enough energy to exploration to ensure its future viability. James March — Organization Science (1991)

Consequences of Imbalance

Too Much Exploration

Over-experimentation, too many unfinished initiatives, financial strain dari R&D tanpa returns. Company tidak extract value dari existing capabilities. Contoh: startup yang continuously pivot tanpa ever monetize product.

Too Much Exploitation

Efficient but ossified. Company menjadi rigid, tidak adapt to environment changes. Classic "innovator's dilemma" (Christensen 1997). Contoh: Nokia/BlackBerry yang terlalu fokus pada existing handset business sementara smartphone revolution terjadi.

Organizational Ambidexterity

Ambidexterity: capability untuk do both exploration + exploitation simultaneously.

Structural Ambidexterity

Separate organizational units untuk exploration vs. exploitation. Exploration unit (R&D, innovation labs) dengan different culture, timeline, success metrics. Exploitation unit (core business) dengan efficiency focus. Contoh: Astra memiliki core mature businesses + exploratory investments (Astra Tol Nusantara, EV investments).

Contextual Ambidexterity

Same units do both—individuals trained to switch between exploration dan exploitation depending on context. Requires cultural sophistication. Contoh: Apple employees bekerja pada existing iPhone improvements sambil develop next-gen products.

Temporal Ambidexterity

Organization cycles between exploration dan exploitation phases. Periods of consolidation (exploitation) alternate with periods of innovation (exploration). Less common but sometimes strategic choice.

Jansen, Vera & Crossan (2009) — Leadership for Ambidexterity

Jansen, Vera & Crossan (Leadership Quarterly 2009) mengintegrasikan exploration-exploitation dengan leadership theory.

Framework

Gambar 14.1 — Jansen, Vera & Crossan Ambidextrous Leadership Framework

Transformational Leadership → Exploration

Why Transformational Drives Exploration

Vision & Inspiration: articulate future possibilities yang menarik followers untuk invest dalam uncertain new directions.

Intellectual Stimulation: challenge assumptions, encourage creative thinking, welcome diverse perspectives.

Idealized Influence: role-model risk-taking dan learning orientation.

Individualized Consideration: support individual development, tolerate failure sebagai learning.

Transformational leaders inspire organization untuk undertake exploration—even when short-term returns unclear.

Transactional Leadership → Exploitation

Why Transactional Drives Exploitation

Clear Goals: specific targets untuk execution excellence.

Contingent Rewards: link performance to rewards—motivates focus pada measurable outcomes.

Management-by-Exception: intervene when standards not met—ensures execution discipline.

Performance Monitoring: track metrics, enforce accountability.

Transactional leaders operationalize strategy—ensure execution pada existing capabilities dengan efficiency.

Environmental Dynamism sebagai Moderator

Jansen et al. finding: leadership style impact dimoderasi oleh environmental dynamism.

High Environmental Dynamism (Hypercompetition)

Exploration is critical—adaptive capabilities diperlukan untuk survive. Transformational leadership memiliki stronger positive impact. Transactional leadership alone insufficient—organization akan tertinggal.

Low Environmental Dynamism (Stable)

Exploitation sufficient—efficiency matters more. Transactional leadership dengan stronger returns. Transformational leadership yang over-emphasize exploration dapat menjadi distraction.

Ambidextrous Leadership Implementation

Single Leader dengan Both Styles

Rare tetapi possible—leaders yang dapat switch style based on context. Contoh: Satya Nadella di Microsoft (transformational untuk cloud pivot, transactional untuk execution).

Complementary TMT Members

Different TMT members dengan different styles—CEO transformational, COO transactional. Requires TMT integration (Chen-Lin-Michel 2010) untuk synergy, bukan conflict.

Level-Specific Leadership

Transformational at higher org levels (strategy), transactional at middle/operational levels (execution). Cascading leadership architecture.

Aplikasi ke Indonesia

Jahja Setiaatmadja di BCA — Balanced Approach

Long-tenure CEO yang shows elements of both. Transformational: digital transformation vision, SMART culture building. Transactional: clear KPIs, consistent performance management, branch network execution discipline. Berada di middle-level environmental dynamism (perbankan moderate)—balanced approach fits.

Andre Soelistyo at GoTo — Transformational (Era Post-Merger)

Facing hypercompetitive environment pasca-merger, needed transformational leadership untuk align Gojek + Tokopedia cultures dan explore new directions (fintech integration, TikTok partnership). Still developing TMT integration.

Ririek Adriansyah di Telkom Indonesia — Transactional

BUMN telco yang operations-heavy. Focus pada operational excellence, execution, performance management. Appropriate untuk relatively stable legacy business sambil exploring 5G + digital adjacencies. TMT complementary members handle exploration.

Pemeriksa Konsep — Minggu 14 (Capstone)

Pemeriksa Konsep · Hypercompetition & Strategic Leadership

K1. D'Aveni's hypercompetition: apakah ini descriptif (semakin banyak industri menjadi hypercompetitive) atau prescriptif (managers harus bertindak as if in hypercompetition)? Konsekuensi untuk Indonesia yang ada industri stable dan industri hypercompetitive?

K2. Chen, Lin & Michel: action aggressiveness × TMT integration. Pilih satu kasus Indonesia di mana aggressive action tanpa TMT integration memberikan hasil negative. Pertahankan.

K3. Jansen et al. ambidextrous leadership. Apakah mungkin one person genuinely ambidextrous? Atau ambidexterity harus di level TMT? Debat dengan contoh.

K4. March exploration-exploitation: apakah ini truly zero-sum tradeoff, atau dapat di-transcend via organizational design? Pertahankan dengan contoh perusahaan Indonesia.

K5. Capstone Integration Question: Pilih satu perusahaan Indonesia. Lakukan full strategic analysis menggunakan minimum 8 kerangka dari 14 minggu mata kuliah. Sintesiskan insights ke single strategic recommendation. Pertahankan dengan rigor akademis.
