③ Article Analysis · Minggu 14

Analisis Artikel 28 — Chen, Lin & Michel (2010)

Judul lengkap: Navigating in a Hypercompetitive Environment: The Roles of Action Aggressiveness and TMT Integration. Penulis: Ming-Jer Chen, Hsiu-Ching Lin, John G. Michel. Publikasi: Strategic Management Journal, Vol. 31 No. 13 (December 2010), pp. 1410–1430. Tipe riset: empirical quantitative—longitudinal analysis dengan data perusahaan publicly traded.

Catatan Sumber Primer

PDF tidak disediakan. Analisis dari abstrak publik + literatur kanonik competitive dynamics + TMT (D'Aveni 1994; Chen & Miller 1994; Hambrick et al. 1996; Ferrier 2001). Mahasiswa dianjurkan mencari PDF asli untuk pendalaman metodologis.

Pertanyaan Riset

Di environments yang hypercompetitive (D'Aveni 1994)—di mana competitive advantages temporary dan competitive interactions aggressive—apa yang menentukan firm performance? Lebih specifically, bagaimana action aggressiveness (frequency + intensity competitive moves) dan TMT integration (integrity fungsi top management team) berinteraksi untuk mempengaruhi kinerja?

Kerangka Teoretis

Chen, Lin & Michel mengintegrasikan:

  • Hypercompetition theory (D'Aveni 1994): competitive advantages temporary, aggressive action critical.
  • Competitive dynamics (Chen & Miller 1994; Ferrier 2001): firms yang take more actions, faster, perform better.
  • Upper echelons theory (Hambrick & Mason 1984): TMT characteristics shape strategic actions.
  • Behavioral theory of the firm (Cyert & March 1963): decision-making processes matter.

Hipotesis

H1 — Action Aggressiveness Positive Impact

Di hypercompetitive environments, firms dengan action aggressiveness lebih tinggi (more frequent, more intense competitive moves) achieve better performance.

H2 — TMT Integration Positive Impact

TMT integration (shared vision, communication, coordination, collaboration) positively impacts firm performance.

H3 — Moderation (Interaksi)

TMT integration memoderasi hubungan action aggressiveness → performance. Dengan TMT integration tinggi, action aggressiveness lebih effectively ditranslate menjadi performance. Dengan TMT fragmented, aggressive actions menjadi counterproductive.

Metode

Sample

Publicly traded firms di industri yang classified sebagai hypercompetitive (tech, computer, electronics). Longitudinal data—multiple years untuk capture dinamika.

Measurement

  • Action aggressiveness: content analysis dari public announcements, press releases—count of competitive actions (pricing, new products, marketing, M&A) and their intensity.
  • TMT integration: survey measures + archival data on TMT composition, tenure, stability, communication patterns.
  • Performance: financial metrics (ROA, market share growth, stock performance).
  • Controls: firm size, age, industry, prior performance.

Analysis

Hierarchical regression untuk test main effects dan interaction. Longitudinal analysis untuk temporal dynamics.

Temuan Utama

Finding 1 — H1 Supported

Action aggressiveness positive associated dengan performance di hypercompetitive environments. Firms yang passive mengalami decline; firms yang aggressive (price moves, product launches, M&A, marketing campaigns) outperform.

Finding 2 — H2 Partially Supported

TMT integration has positive main effect—firms dengan integrated TMT outperform fragmented TMT. Effect size moderate tetapi statistically significant.

Finding 3 — H3 Strongly Supported

Interaction effect significant: action aggressiveness × TMT integration. Firms dengan HIGH action aggressiveness + HIGH TMT integration = highest performance. Firms dengan HIGH action aggressiveness + LOW TMT integration = worst performance. TMT integration is crucial moderator—tanpa integration, aggressive actions menjadi destructive.

Finding 4 — Implication for Passive Firms

Firms yang passive (low action aggressiveness) perform worse than aggressive firms regardless of TMT integration. Dalam hypercompetition, passivity = slow death.

Kontribusi Teoretis

1. Integrasi Competitive Dynamics + TMT Research

Literatur competitive dynamics traditionally fokus pada firm-level actions. Literatur TMT fokus pada management characteristics. Chen et al. menunjukkan bahwa keduanya interact—action aggressiveness effectiveness bergantung pada TMT capability untuk coordinate dan execute.

2. Nuance untuk "Aggressive Action" Prescription

Literatur hypercompetition (D'Aveni, Ferrier) cenderung merekomendasikan aggressive action universally. Chen et al. memberi nuance: aggressive action harus didukung TMT integration. Otherwise, prescription becomes counterproductive.

3. Empirical Validation for D'Aveni

Memberi bukti empiris quantitative untuk klaim D'Aveni tentang pentingnya aggressive competitive maneuvering di hypercompetitive environments.

Keterbatasan

  • US-centric sample: findings mungkin berbeda di emerging markets dengan institutional voids, family-dominated firms, atau state-owned enterprises.
  • Focus pada financial performance: tidak mengukur non-financial outcomes (stakeholder engagement, innovation capability).
  • Measurement challenges untuk TMT integration: relying on survey + archival proxies—subjective elements.
  • Temporal scope: findings dari period spesifik yang might not generalize ke different competitive landscapes.

Aplikasi ke Indonesia

Ride-Hailing Triopoly: Testing Chen-Lin-Michel Framework

GoTo, Grab, ShopeeFood—semua aggressive dalam competitive actions (pricing, promotions, new features, strategic alliances). Success differences likely correlate dengan TMT integration quality:

  • GoTo post-merger facing TMT integration challenge (Gojek + Tokopedia cultures).
  • Grab dengan relatively stable senior leadership (Anthony Tan sebagai CEO since founding).
  • ShopeeFood sebagai part of Sea Group dengan clear leadership chain.
Empirical prediction: firms dengan better TMT integration akan outperform pada medium-term basis, meskipun semua menjalankan aggressive actions.

E-Commerce Shakeout

Tokopedia, Shopee, Lazada, Bukalapak—semua hypercompetitive environment. Bukalapak post-shakeout struggle likely correlate dengan combination of reduced aggressiveness (slow pivot) + TMT challenges (management changes, investor pressure). Tokopedia-TikTok merger tested TMT integration lintas-organizations.

Banking Digital Transformation

Perbankan Indonesia dalam transition phase—industries transitioning to more hypercompetitive. BCA Jahja Setiaatmadja represents HIGH TMT integration. Bank Mandiri post-merger complex TMT. Bank Jago agile TMT with startup culture. Empirical test: which leadership+action combination outperform over next 5-10 years?

Pertanyaan Diskusi

Diskusi

Pilih satu industri hypercompetitive Indonesia. Identifikasi 3-4 major players. Estimasi masing-masing pada dua dimensi: (a) action aggressiveness (berapa aggressive competitive moves?), (b) TMT integration (berapa integrated leadership?). Predict relative performance berdasarkan Chen-Lin-Michel framework. Validate dengan bukti public yang available.

Analisis Artikel 29 — Jansen, Vera & Crossan (2009)

Judul lengkap: Strategic Leadership for Exploration and Exploitation: The Moderating Role of Environmental Dynamism. Penulis: Justin J. P. Jansen, Dusya Vera, Mary Crossan. Publikasi: The Leadership Quarterly, Vol. 20 No. 1 (February 2009), pp. 5–18. Tipe riset: empirical quantitative—survey-based dengan hierarchical linear modeling.

Catatan Sumber Primer

PDF tidak disediakan. Analisis dari abstrak publik + literatur kanonik leadership + ambidexterity (Bass 1985; March 1991; Tushman & O'Reilly 1996; Jansen et al. 2006). Mahasiswa dianjurkan mencari PDF asli.

Pertanyaan Riset

Bagaimana different leadership styles (transformational vs. transactional) mempengaruhi organizational exploration vs. exploitation? Apakah dampak leadership style dimoderasi oleh environmental dynamism?

Kerangka Teoretis

Integrasi tiga literatur:

1. Leadership Theory (Bass 1985)

Transformational leadership: vision, inspirational motivation, intellectual stimulation, individualized consideration.

Transactional leadership: contingent rewards, management-by-exception (active and passive).

2. Exploration-Exploitation (March 1991)

Exploration: search for new possibilities, variation, experimentation.
Exploitation: refinement, efficiency, selection of known alternatives.

3. Environmental Dynamism

Degree of change dan instability di industry environment—rate of product/service innovation, technology change, customer preference shifts, competitor actions.

Hipotesis

H1 — Transformational → Exploration

Transformational leadership positively related to exploration. Vision + inspiration + intellectual stimulation foster novel thinking and experimentation.

H2 — Transactional → Exploitation

Transactional leadership positively related to exploitation. Clear goals + contingent rewards foster efficiency and execution of existing strategies.

H3a — Dynamism Moderates Transformational-Exploration

Relationship between transformational leadership dan exploration stronger di high dynamism (change-intensive) environments. Under dynamism, exploration is more critical for survival, and transformational leadership capitalizes this.

H3b — Dynamism Moderates Transactional-Exploitation

Relationship between transactional leadership dan exploitation stronger di low dynamism (stable) environments. Under stability, exploitation is sufficient, and transactional leadership optimally fits.

Metode

Sample

Survey sample dari organizations di various industries. Multi-source data—CEOs rate own leadership, subordinates rate exploration/exploitation activities, independent measures of environmental dynamism.

Measurement

  • Leadership styles: Multifactor Leadership Questionnaire (MLQ) subscales.
  • Exploration & Exploitation: Jansen et al. (2006) scales.
  • Environmental dynamism: Dess & Beard (1984) scales—rate of change in technology, competitors, customer preferences.

Analysis

Hierarchical linear regression to test main effects dan interaction effects. Controlled untuk firm size, age, industry.

Temuan Utama

Finding 1 — H1 Supported

Transformational leadership significantly positively related to exploration. Leaders yang articulate vision + stimulate intellectually encourage organization untuk explore new possibilities.

Finding 2 — H2 Supported

Transactional leadership significantly positively related to exploitation. Leaders yang set clear goals + provide contingent rewards foster execution dari existing strategies.

Finding 3 — H3a Supported

Dynamism strengthens transformational leadership → exploration relationship. Under high change, transformational leadership truly valuable untuk driving exploration.

Finding 4 — H3b Supported

Dynamism weakens transactional leadership → exploitation relationship (i.e., dynamism strengthens transformational need). In high-dynamism environments, transactional leadership alone insufficient—organization needs exploration alongside exploitation.

Finding 5 — Ambidextrous Need in Dynamic Environments

Di dynamic environments, organizations ideally combine transformational (for exploration) and transactional (for exploitation) leadership. Single-style leadership insufficient.

Kontribusi Teoretis

1. Linkages Leadership-Ambidexterity

Previous ambidexterity research focused pada organizational structure (Tushman & O'Reilly 1996). Jansen et al. introduce leadership dimension—how leaders enable or inhibit ambidexterity.

2. Contextual Leadership Theory

Challenges "one best leadership style" narratives. Different styles optimal di different contexts. Validates contingency perspective.

3. Practical Implications

CEO development, TMT composition, succession planning—harus consider environmental dynamism dan balance antara transformational + transactional styles.

Keterbatasan

  • Cross-sectional data: dapat suggest correlation tetapi kausalitas tidak fully established.
  • Survey-based: leadership styles self-reported oleh CEOs—potential social desirability bias.
  • Sample concentration: Western firms (Netherlands + North America)—generalizability ke emerging markets uncertain.
  • Simplification: transformational-transactional dichotomy mungkin oversimplify leadership complexity.

Aplikasi ke Indonesia

Case 1 — Nadiem Makarim Era di Gojek (2010-2019)

Environmental dynamism: sangat tinggi—emerging ride-hailing industry, rapid technology change, shifting regulasi.
Leadership style: predominantly transformational—articulating vision "empower Indonesia through technology", intellectual stimulation untuk engineer team.
Exploration: tinggi—continuous new verticals (GoFood, GoSend, GoPay, etc.).
Fit: strong fit dengan Jansen framework—transformational × high dynamism → strong exploration. Hasil: rapid growth, category creation.

Case 2 — Jahja Setiaatmadja di BCA

Environmental dynamism: moderate (perbankan Indonesia—stable regulatory but increasing digital disruption).
Leadership style: mix transformational + transactional. Transformational dimensions: SMART culture building, digital transformation vision. Transactional: clear performance metrics, disciplined execution.
Exploration + Exploitation: balanced. Mobile banking development (exploration) + branch efficiency optimization (exploitation).
Fit: consistent dengan ambidextrous leadership hypothesis. Moderate dynamism rewards balanced approach.

Case 3 — BUMN Legacy Leadership

Banyak BUMN Indonesia secara historis lebih transactional—operational focus, execution discipline, less vision articulation. Consistent dengan less dynamic environments (regulated utilities, state-mandated roles). Tetapi ketika environment berubah (energy transition, digital economy), BUMN yang gagal shift menuju transformational leadership mengalami decline relative ke private sector competitors.

Case 4 — Family Conglomerate Transitions

Second/third generation transitions di konglomerat Indonesia (Astra, Salim, Djarum, Sinar Mas) adalah moment of leadership test. Founder-generation cenderung transformational (building conglomerate). Second generation sering transactional (professionalizing operations). Third generation challenges: reconfigure untuk digital era—need transformational leadership again.

Pertanyaan Diskusi

Diskusi

Pilih satu perusahaan Indonesia. Assess:

  • Environmental dynamism yang dihadapi (low/medium/high).
  • Current leadership style (predominantly transformational / transactional / mixed).
  • Current balance exploration-exploitation.
  • Apakah leadership style fit dengan environment? Jika tidak, apa rekomendasi?
Gunakan Jansen et al. framework untuk sistematis analysis.

④ Indonesian Company Examples · Minggu 14

GoTo-Grab-ShopeeFood Triopoly — Hypercompetition Indonesia yang Hidup

Jangkar konsep: hypercompetition D'Aveni; action aggressiveness × TMT integration (Chen-Lin-Michel); temporary advantages; Indonesia sebagai battleground regional yang hypercompetitive.

Industri food delivery dan mobility Indonesia adalah salah satu contoh paling vivid dari hypercompetitive environment yang dibahas D'Aveni. Tiga pemain besar—GoTo (Gojek, dari Indonesia), Grab (dari Singapura/Malaysia), dan ShopeeFood (dari Shopee/Sea Group Singapura)—bersaing dalam cara yang hampir tidak ada precedent dalam strategic management literature Indonesia.

The Triopoly — Hypercompetition Indonesia

GoTo (IDX: GOTO) · Grab Singapore · Sea Group (Shopee)
3 playersMajor competitors locked in battleIndustry observation 2021–2024
Multi-verticalRide + Food + Delivery + PaymentPlatform business models
TemporaryAdvantages—eroded quicklyD'Aveni hypercompetition framework

Four Arena Analysis (D'Aveni)

1. Cost & Quality Arena

Ketiga player memiliki scale yang sama dan costs yang similar. Product quality relatively comparable—all three can deliver food, arrange rides, enable payment dengan quality serupa. Cost/quality arena menjadi price war zone—discounts, promos, subsidies.

2. Timing & Know-How Arena

Gojek first-mover di Indonesia (2010—driver ojek digitization). Grab follower dari 2014 (regional Southeast Asia play). ShopeeFood 2021 last entrant but leveraging Shopee ecosystem. First-mover advantage (Gojek) eroded karena Grab dan ShopeeFood learn dan compete aggressively.

3. Strongholds Arena

GoTo strongest di Jakarta/Indonesia major cities. Grab strongest di Southeast Asia regional. ShopeeFood leveraging Shopee e-commerce user base. No player has unassailable stronghold—each faces competition di their supposed strongholds.

4. Deep Pockets Arena

All three backed by massive capital (GoTo listed, Grab listed via SPAC, Sea Group listed). Deep pockets menjadi table stakes, not competitive advantage. Financial discipline (path to profitability) menjadi new battleground pasca 2022 Fed rate hikes.

Action Aggressiveness — Frekuensi dan Intensitas

Semua tiga menunjukkan extreme action aggressiveness:

Pricing Wars

Ride subsidies, food delivery promo codes, payment cashbacks. Setiap player respond cepat pada competitor moves. Konsumen Indonesia terbiasa membandingkan tiga apps untuk harga terbaik—fueling aggression.

Product Launches

Continuous new features—subscription services (GoClub, GrabUnlimited), premium tiers, new verticals (grocery, cloud kitchens, financial services). Each player announces major launches multiple times per year.

Strategic Alliances

GoTo merger dengan Tokopedia (2021); GoTo-TikTok Shop partnership (2024). Grab partnerships dengan banks (for fintech). ShopeeFood leveraging full Sea Group ecosystem. Each alliance reshuffles competitive dynamics.

M&A Activity

GoTo-Tokopedia mega-merger adalah industry-reshaping move. Grab SPAC listing brought massive capital. Sea Group continuously acquire dan invest in adjacent businesses.

TMT Integration — Variabel Kritis (Chen-Lin-Michel)

Berdasarkan public information:

GoTo — TMT Integration Challenge

Post-merger Gojek + Tokopedia menciptakan TMT integration challenge. Different cultures (Gojek's "tech ops" culture vs. Tokopedia's "marketplace" culture), different leadership styles. CEO transitions (Andre Soelistyo → Patrick Walujo 2023) menunjukkan TMT dynamics yang evolving. Efforts to integrate sedang berjalan.

Implication (Chen-Lin-Michel): aggressive actions GoTo may be sub-optimized by TMT integration gaps. Post-integration maturity akan determine future performance.

Grab — Founder Leadership Continuity

Anthony Tan as CEO since founding 2012—long-tenure leadership continuity. TMT relatively stable. Clear vision + execution. TMT integration likely stronger dari GoTo.

Implication: Grab's aggressive actions likely better coordinated—but regional scope adds complexity (each country operation dengan different dynamics).

ShopeeFood (Sea Group) — Integrated Ecosystem

ShopeeFood sebagai part of larger Sea Group (Shopee e-commerce + Garena gaming + SeaMoney fintech). Forrest Li sebagai CEO dari Sea. Strong vertical integration dan clear ecosystem logic. TMT integration benefits dari single parent company structure.

Implication: ShopeeFood dapat leverage cross-ecosystem actions dengan TMT coordination yang smooth—but also facing Sea Group broader financial pressures.

Temporary Advantages — Evidence

Bukti hypercompetition:

  • Pricing: lead changes frequent. Satu player lower price, competitors follow within days. Pricing advantage temporary.
  • Product features: new features (loyalty programs, subscription tiers, etc.) replicated by competitors within months.
  • Brand positioning: perception of "which is better app" fluctuates year-over-year.
  • Market share: shifts rapidly based on current marketing campaigns.

Di industri ini, sustainable competitive advantage adalah illusion—as D'Aveni predicted.

Strategic Implications — Capstone Insights

1. Traditional Strategic Frameworks Limited

Porter Five Forces analysis reveal persistent challenges. VRIN analysis shows few truly inimitable resources. Generic strategies (cost vs. differentiation) overlap. Traditional frameworks under-predict dinamika industri ini.

2. Dynamic Capabilities Critical

Firms yang survive akan memiliki strong dynamic capabilities (Teece)—ability sensing, seizing, transforming. Continuous adaptation bukan episodic change.

3. Business Model Innovation Required

Minggu 12 business model innovation frameworks highly relevant. GoTo super-app model, Grab regional model, ShopeeFood ecosystem model—each distinctive. Continuous innovation required.

4. Stakeholder Capabilities Matter

Minggu 13 stakeholder capability enhancement relevant. Platforms yang genuinely enhance driver/merchant/consumer capabilities build cooperative advantage yang sulit direplikasi.

5. Leadership Integration Decisive

Chen-Lin-Michel framework suggests: di hypercompetitive Indonesia, TMT integration quality akan likely determine long-term winner among triopoly—bukan aggressive action level (semua aggressive).

Capstone Reflection

Analisis triopoly ini mengintegrasikan:

  • Minggu 3 (external environment): hypercompetition extreme case.
  • Minggu 4 (dynamic capabilities): critical capability.
  • Minggu 5-7 (strategy formulation): strategic generics break down.
  • Minggu 8 (international): regional competition (Grab regional, Sea regional).
  • Minggu 11 (execution): TMT integration prerequisite.
  • Minggu 12 (business model innovation): different models compete.
  • Minggu 13 (stakeholder): platform businesses inherently stakeholder-based.
  • Minggu 14 (hypercompetition + leadership): central concept.

Untuk UAS: kemampuan mengintegrasikan frameworks untuk kasus seperti ini adalah inti dari strategic management sophistication.

Sidebar 1 — Jahja Setiaatmadja di BCA: Long-Tenure Strategic Leadership

Jangkar konsep: contextual leadership—balanced transformational-transactional style dalam moderate-dynamism environment; TMT integration yang dibangun via continuity + internal culture; contrast to high-turnover leadership.

Jahja Setiaatmadja sebagai Presdir BCA sejak 2011—lebih dari 13 tahun continuity. Ini anomaly dalam Indonesian banking industri yang sering mengalami CEO turnover. Strategic implications dari continuity ini warrant careful analysis.

Environmental Dynamism Context

Perbankan konsumer Indonesia dari Jansen et al. perspective:

  • Historis (pre-2015): relatively low dynamism. Regulated industry, clear competitors (Big-4 banks), stable consumer behavior.
  • Recent (2015+): increasing dynamism. Digital banks emerging (Bank Jago, SeaBank, Allo), fintech challengers, changing consumer preferences, QRIS standardization.

BCA berada di industry yang transitioning from stable toward more dynamic.

Jahja's Leadership Style Analysis

Transformational Elements

  • Vision articulation: "bank pilihan utama andalan masyarakat" consistent dan diperkuat.
  • Intellectual stimulation: encouraging digital transformation, fostering BDP talent untuk innovative thinking.
  • Idealized influence: respected public figure, role model untuk banking professional integrity.
  • Individualized consideration: known untuk personal connection dengan senior executives.

Transactional Elements

  • Clear performance metrics: CASA ratio, NPL, ROE tracked rigorously.
  • Contingent rewards: BCA known untuk performance-based compensation.
  • Management-by-exception: intervention saat KPI tidak tercapai.
  • Performance monitoring: robust regular reviews.

Balanced / Ambidextrous Leadership

Jahja exemplifies balanced style—not purely one or the other. Consistent dengan Jansen et al. hypothesis: moderate dynamism rewards balanced leadership. Dalam high dynamism, pure transformational needed; dalam pure stability, pure transactional sufficient; dalam between, balance wins.

TMT Integration Consequences

Long-tenure CEO + culture of internal promotion = extremely integrated TMT:

  • TMT members grew up together, trust established over decades.
  • Shared mental models (same training, same culture).
  • Predictable decision processes.
  • Lower politics karena tenure stability.

Consequence: decision-making cepat, execution coherent, aggressive actions effectively coordinated when taken. Contoh: digital transformation BCA (BCA Mobile, Welma, OneKlik, QRIS integration) berjalan cepat dan coherent.

Debate — Continuity vs. Fresh Perspective

Pro-Continuity Arguments

  • Deep institutional knowledge.
  • Established relationships.
  • Predictable strategic direction.
  • TMT integration benefits.

Concerns about Continuity

  • Risk of strategic persistence (upper echelons theory—long tenure = commit to status quo).
  • Fresh perspective limited.
  • Succession risk—what happens post-Jahja?
  • Adaptation capability if environment becomes much more dynamic.

BCA's approach: continuity with pipeline development. BDP (Banker Development Program) continuously grooming next generation leaders. This is conscious succession management, bukan just accident.

Sidebar 2 — Telkom TMT: BUMN Ambidextrous Challenge

Jangkar konsep: BUMN legacy TMT menghadapi transformasi digital; contextual ambidexterity requirement; exploration (5G, cloud, enterprise digital) + exploitation (legacy connectivity, fixed broadband); governance complexity.

Telkom Indonesia (IDX: TLKM) adalah case interesting untuk analisis ambidextrous leadership di konteks BUMN. Perusahaan memiliki:

  • Legacy business yang matang (fixed line, broadband)—need exploitation.
  • Growth segments (enterprise digital, cloud, data center, 5G mobile)—need exploration.
  • Ownership pemerintah dengan policy mandates—adding complexity to leadership dynamics.

Environmental Dynamism

Telekomunikasi Indonesia:

  • Mature segments (mobile voice, SMS): low dynamism, declining demand.
  • Evolving segments (data, mobile internet): moderate dynamism.
  • Emerging segments (5G, enterprise cloud, IoT, AI services): high dynamism.

Telkom operates across all three simultaneously—maximal dynamism variance.

TMT Structure dan Ambidextrous Challenges

BUMN Governance Layer

Dewan Komisaris appointed via government process. Dewan Direksi mix of professional + government-influenced appointments. This layered structure dapat create TMT fragmentation antara professional management objectives (return on investment) dan government mandates (national development, employment, connectivity targets).

CEO Tenure Typically Shorter

BUMN CEOs appointed 5-year terms, sometimes renewed. Compared to Jahja at BCA (13+ years), BUMN leadership continuity lower. Implication: TMT integration harder to build, strategic direction shifts dengan administrasi changes.

Ambidextrous Requirements

Telkom requires:

  • Exploitation leadership untuk legacy operations (transactional—clear KPIs, operational excellence, cost management).
  • Exploration leadership untuk digital growth (transformational—vision untuk digital future, intellectual stimulation, risk tolerance).
Challenge: finding leaders yang dapat do both, atau TMT yang complementary.

Strategic Responses — Structural Ambidexterity

Telkom's approach: structural separation:

  • Core legacy operations under Telkom main company—transactional leadership.
  • Digital subsidiaries (Telkomsel—mobile, Metranet—enterprise, Telkomsat—satellite, Indico—digital platforms, TelkomSigma—IT)—each with dedicated leadership focused on their domain.
  • Mitratel (menara)—separated, IPO'd untuk financial independence.

This creates multiple TMT layers—complex tetapi dapat enable ambidexterity.

Leadership Challenges

1. Speed of Decisions

BUMN governance + multiple subsidiaries = slow decision-making. Di industri dengan dynamism meningkat, speed matters. Telkom's response: delegated authorities, empowered subsidiary leadership.

2. Talent Competition

Digital tech talent preferred private sector (GoTo, Bank Jago, startups). BUMN compensation structures kurang kompetitif. Telkom's response: subsidiary-level compensation flexibility, partnerships (Telkomsel with Singtel, etc.).

3. Political-Commercial Balance

BUMN harus balance national development mandates dengan commercial returns. This inherently creates TMT tensions between different objective functions. Integration requires skilled leadership yang dapat articulate how these can align.

Kontras Tiga Flagship Minggu 14

ContohEnvironmentLeadership StyleTMT Integration
GoTo-Grab-ShopeeFoodHypercompetitiveVariable (founder vs. professional)Variable—TMT integration differentiator
Jahja di BCAModerate dynamismBalanced (transformational + transactional)Extremely high (long tenure + internal promotion)
Telkom TMTMixed (hi/low dynamism)Needs ambidextrousChallenged by BUMN structure complexity

Ketiga menunjukkan spectrum:

  • Hypercompetition: demands integrated aggressive TMT.
  • Moderate dynamism: rewards balanced leadership + continuity.
  • Legacy + emerging mix: requires structural ambidexterity.

Pelajaran Strategic Leadership Capstone

1. Leadership Style Must Match Environment

Jansen et al. dan Chen-Lin-Michel converge: context matters. No "one best leadership". Leaders harus assess environment dan calibrate style.

2. TMT Integration adalah Multiplier

Good leadership amplified oleh integrated TMT; weakened oleh fragmentation. Building TMT integration adalah long-term investment.

3. Succession Matters

Long-tenure continuity (Jahja BCA) benefits present but creates succession risk. Short tenure (some BUMN) creates integration challenges. Intentional succession planning crucial.

4. Organizational Structure Supports Leadership

Structural ambidexterity (Telkom separated digital subsidiaries) enables different leadership styles where appropriate. Organization design is leadership design.

Final Capstone Reflection

Minggu 14 menutup mata kuliah dengan dua tema integratif. Hypercompetition forces us to reconsider classical strategy assumptions. Strategic leadership determines whether organization can actually translate strategy into outcomes. Together, they remind us: strategic management is ultimately about people making complex choices under uncertainty—frameworks help, but judgment, integration, and leadership execution determine success.

Selamat menyiapkan UAS.

Catatan Verifikasi

Analisis triopoly, leadership styles, dan TMT dynamics didasarkan pada public information—annual reports, press releases, industry reports, media coverage. Beberapa claims tentang TMT integration (misalnya "TMT integration challenges at GoTo") adalah inference dari publicly observable signals (CEO transitions, merger dinamika) bukan dari internal organizational assessments. Mahasiswa dianjurkan verifikasi dari ir.gotocompany.com, investor.grab.com, sea.com/investor, bca.co.id/id/investor, telkom.co.id/en/investor-relations.

Catatan Akhir

Catatan Metodologis

Master Course Companion ini dirakit dari 14 minggu materi pembelajaran MST304, setara dengan 55+ halaman HTML individu yang juga tersedia sebagai unit mandiri di folder course-materials/outputs/. Dokumen ini dirancang untuk studi intensif terstruktur—membaca secara berurutan dari Minggu 1 sampai Minggu 14, atau sebagai referensi komprehensif untuk persiapan UAS.

Setiap minggu mengikuti arsitektur empat-bagian yang konsisten:

  • ① Study Guide / Aid — panduan belajar: urutan membaca, konsep inti, koneksi antar-minggu, fokus diskusi + self-check questions.
  • ② Main Summary / Ebook — sintesis akademik lengkap dengan framework diagrams (SVG inline), bold key terms, concept-check callouts, referensi.
  • ③ Article Analysis — kajian mendalam artikel empiris (Art.1–4 dengan PDF; Art.5–29 berbasis abstrak publik + literatur kanonik dengan disclosure banner).
  • ④ Indonesian Company Examples — flagship yang dianalisis mendalam + 1–2 sidebar komparatif, dengan tabel sumber dan catatan verifikasi.

Disiplin Sumber

Seluruh data Indonesian company example didasarkan pada materi publik yang diungkapkan perusahaan: annual report, sustainability report, disclosure IDX/OJK, investor relations materials, publikasi regulator (OJK, Kementerian BUMN, Kemenkominfo, dll.). Setiap data point menyertakan document type + tahun. Di mana angka tidak dapat secara jelas dirujuk, digunakan bahasa deskriptif ("among top-3 by revenue") alih-alih angka buatan. Mahasiswa dianjurkan memverifikasi angka terkini dari pengajuan aktual sebelum menggunakan dalam tugas akhir atau tesis.
